\\n403: /// Asserts that two expressions are equal to each other (using [`PartialEq`]).\\n404: ///\\n405: /// On panic, this macro will print the values of the expressions with their\\n406: /// [`Debug`] or [`ToString`] representations with a colorized diff of the\\n407: /// changes in the debug output.  It picks [`Debug`] for all types that are\\n408: /// not strings themselves and [`ToString`] for [`str`] and [`String`].\\n409: ///\\n410: /// Like [`assert!`], this macro has a second form, where a custom panic\\n411: /// message can be provided.\\n412: ///\\n413: /// ```rust\\n414: /// use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\\n415: /// assert_eq!((1..3).collect::<Vec<_>>(), vec![1, 2]);\\n416: /// ```\\n417: #[macro_export]\\n418: macro_rules! assert_eq {\\n419:     ($left_label:ident: $left:expr, $right_label:ident: $right:expr $(,)?) => ({\\n420:         $crate::__assert_eq!(make_diff, $left_label, $left, $right_label, $right, \\\"\\\");\\n421:     });\\n422:     ($left_label:ident: $left:expr, $right_label:ident: $right:expr, $($arg:tt)*) => ({\\n423:         $crate::__assert_eq!(make_diff, $left_label, $left, $right_label, $right, format_args!(\\\": {}\\\", format_args!($($arg)*)));\\n424:     });\\n425:     ($left:expr, $right:expr $(,)?) => ({\\n426:         $crate::assert_eq!(left: $left, right: $right);\\n427:     });\\n428:     ($left:expr, $right:expr, $($arg:tt)*) => ({\\n429:         $crate::assert_eq!(left: $left, right: $right, $($arg)*);\\n430:     });\\n431: }\\n432: \\n433: /// Deprecated macro. On failed assertions it renders out a colorized diff to the terminal.\\n4: //!\\n5: //! It comes with a handful of macros to replace [`std::assert_eq!`] with:\\n6: //!\\n7: //! - [`assert_eq!`]: diffs `Debug` on assertion failure.\\n8: #![cfg_attr(\\n9:     feature = \\\"serde\\\",\\n10:     doc = r#\\\"\\n11: - [`assert_serde_eq!`]: diffs `Serialize` on assertion failure.\\n12: \\\"#\\n13: )]\\n14: //!\\n15: //! ![](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mitsuhiko/similar-asserts/main/assets/screenshot.png)\\n16: //!\\n17: //! # Usage\\n18: //!\\n19: //! ```rust\\n20: //! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\\n21: //! assert_eq!((1..3).collect::<Vec<_>>(), vec![1, 2]);\\n22: //! ```\\n23: //!\\n24: //! This crate works best if you add it as `dev-dependency` only.  To make your code\n40: //! still compile you can use conditional uses that override the default uses for the\n41: //! `assert_eq!` macro from the stdlib:\n42: //!\n43: //! ```\n44: //! #[cfg(test)]\n45: //! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\n46: //! ```\n47: //!\n48: //! Since `similar_asserts` uses the `similar` library for diffing you can also\n49: //! enable optimziation for them in all build types for quicker diffing.  Add\n50: //! this to your `Cargo.toml`:\n51: //!\n52: //! ```toml\n53: //! [profile.dev.package.similar]\n54: //! opt-level = 3\n55: //! ```\n56: //!\n57: //! # String Truncation\n58: //!\n59: //! By default the assertion only shows 200 characters.  This can be changed with the\n60: //! `SIMILAR_ASSERTS_MAX_STRING_LENGTH` environment variable.  Setting it to `0` disables\n61: //! all truncation, otherwise it sets the maximum number of characters before truncation\n62: //! kicks in.\n63: //!\n64: //! # Manual Diff Printing\n65: //!\n66: //! If you want to build your own comparison macros and you need a quick and simple\n67: //! way to render diffs, you can use the [`SimpleDiff`] type and display it:\n68: //!\n69: //! ```should_panic\n70: //! use similar_asserts::SimpleDiff;\n71: //! panic!(\"Not equal\\n\\n{}\", SimpleDiff::from_str(\"a\\nb\\n\", \"b\\nb\\n\", \"left\", \"right\"));\n72: //! ```\n73: use std::borrow::Cow;\n74: use std::fmt::{self, Display};\n75: use std::time::Duration;\n76: \n77: use console::{style, Style};\n78: use similar::{Algorithm, ChangeTag, TextDiff};\n79: \n80: #[cfg(feature = \"serde\")]\n81: #[doc(hidden)]\n82: pub mod serde_impl;\n83: \n84: // This needs to be public as we are using it internally in a macro.\n85: #[doc(hidden)]\n86: pub mod print;\n87: \n88: /// The maximum number of characters a string can be long before truncating.\n89: fn get_max_string_length() -> usize {\n90:     use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicUsize, Ordering};\n91:     static TRUNCATE: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(!0);\n92:     let rv = TRUNCATE.load(Ordering::Relaxed);\n93:     if rv != !0 {\n94:         return rv;\n95:     }\n96:     let rv: usize = std::env::var(\"SIMILAR_ASSERTS_MAX_STRING_LENGTH\")\n97:         .ok()\n98:         .and_then(|x| x.parse().ok())\n99:         .unwrap_or(200);\n100:     TRUNCATE.store(rv, Ordering::Relaxed);\n101:     rv\n102: }\n103: \n104: /// A console printable diff.\n105: ///\n106: /// The [`Display`](std::fmt::Display) implementation of this type renders out a\n107: /// diff with ANSI markers so it creates a nice colored diff. This can be used to\n108: /// build your own custom assertions in addition to the ones from this crate.\n109: ///\n110: /// It does not provide much customization beyond what's possible done by default.\n111: pub struct SimpleDiff<'a> {\n112:     pub(crate) left_short: Cow<'a, str>,\n113:     pub(crate) right_short: Cow<'a, str>,\n114:     pub(crate) left_expanded: Option<Cow<'a, \n236: fn trailing_newline(s: &str) -> &str {\n237:     if s.ends_with(\"\\r\\n\") {\n238:         \"\\r\\n\"\n239:     } else if s.ends_with(\"\\r\") {\n240:         \"\\r\"\n241:     } else if \\n313: /// Asserts that two expressions are equal to each other (using [`PartialEq`]) using [`Serialize`](serde::Serialize) for comparision.\\n314: ///\\n315: /// On panic, this macro will print the values of the expressions with their\\n316: /// serde [`Serialize`](serde::Serialize) representations rendered in the same\\n317: /// format that [`std::fmt::Debug`] would with a colorized diff of the ```rust\\n324: /// use similar_asserts::assert_serde_eq;\\n325: /// assert_serde_eq!((1..3).collect::<Vec<_>>(), vec![1, 2]);\\n326: /// ```\\n327: ///\\n328: /// This requires the `serde`
